1191 #ifdef anatree_cxx
1192 anatree::anatree(TTree *tree) : fChain(0)
1193 {
1194 // if parameter tree is not specified (or zero), connect the file
1195 // used to generate this class and read the Tree.
1196  if (tree == 0) {
1197  TFile *f = (TFile*)gROOT->GetListOfFiles()->FindObject("../../../files/mcreco_ana_hist.root");
1198  if (!f || !f->IsOpen()) {
1199  f = new TFile("../../../files/mcreco_ana_hist.root");
1200  }
1201  TDirectory * dir = (TDirectory*)f->Get("../../../files/mcreco_ana_hist.root:/analysistree");
1202  dir->GetObject("anatree",tree);
1203 
1204  }
1205  Init(tree);
1206 }
1207 
1208 anatree::~anatree()
1209 {
1210  if (!fChain) return;
1211  delete fChain->GetCurrentFile();
1212 }
1213 
1214 Int_t anatree::GetEntry(Long64_t entry)
1215 {
1216 // Read contents of entry.
1217  if (!fChain) return 0;
1218  return fChain->GetEntry(entry);
1219 }
1220 Long64_t anatree::LoadTree(Long64_t entry)
1221 {
1222 // Set the environment to read one entry
1223  if (!fChain) return -5;
1224  Long64_t centry = fChain->LoadTree(entry);
1225  if (centry < 0) return centry;
1226  if (fChain->GetTreeNumber() != fCurrent) {
1227  fCurrent = fChain->GetTreeNumber();
1228  Notify();
1229  }
1230  return centry;
1231 }
1232 
1233 void anatree::Init(TTree *tree)
1234 {
1235  // The Init() function is called when the selector needs to initialize
1236  // a new tree or chain. Typically here the branch addresses and branch
1237  // pointers of the tree will be set.
1238  // It is normally not necessary to make changes to the generated
1239  // code, but the routine can be extended by the user if needed.
1240  // Init() will be called many times when running on PROOF
1241  // (once per file to be processed).
1242 
1243  // Set object pointer
1244  processname = 0;
1245  mctrk_Process = 0;
1246  mctrk_MotherProcess = 0;
1247  mctrk_AncesotorProcess = 0;
1248  // Set branch addresses and branch pointers
1249  if (!tree) return;
1250  fChain = tree;
1251  fCurrent = -1;
1252  fChain->SetMakeClass(1);
1253 
1254  fChain->SetBranchAddress("run", &run, &b_run);
1255  fChain->SetBranchAddress("subrun", &subrun, &b_subrun);

1825 
1826 Bool_t anatree::Notify()
1827 {
1828  // The Notify() function is called when a new file is opened. This
1829  // can be either for a new TTree in a TChain or when when a new TTree
1830  // is started when using PROOF. It is normally not necessary to make changes
1831  // to the generated code, but the routine can be extended by the
1832  // user if needed. The return value is currently not used.
1833 
1834  return kTRUE;
1835 }
1836 
1837 void anatree::Show(Long64_t entry)
1838 {
1839 // Print contents of entry.
1840 // If entry is not specified, print current entry
1841  if (!fChain) return;
1842  fChain->Show(entry);
1843 }
1844 Int_t anatree::Cut(Long64_t entry)
1845 {
1846 // This function may be called from Loop.
1847 // returns 1 if entry is accepted.
1848 // returns -1 otherwise.
1849  return 1;
1850 }
